<initial_plan>

1) **Hard Constraints**
- Location: Toronto.
- Property type: Condo (1–2 bedrooms).
- Budget: CAD $420,000–$480,000 total.
- Must have potential for a creative workspace (e.g., home office/studio area).
- Financing must be joint (user + Alex).

2) **Soft Constraints**
- Preference for modern design and good natural lighting.
- Preference for move-in ready condition.
- Desire for nearby amenities (transit, shops, etc.).
- Legal, moving, and setup services can be flexible depending on cost.

3) **Task Decomposition**
- **Step 1:** Identify both buyers (user + Alex) and confirm their joint purchasing intent.
- **Step 2:** Query the external agent (real estate agent) for suitable condos in Toronto that fit the criteria.
- **Step 3:** Request financing and mortgage options (joint ownership) within the specified budget from banks or lenders.
- **Step 4:** Find legal services (real estate lawyer, title search, closing costs).
- **Step 5:** Estimate moving and setup services (movers, utilities, internet, etc.).
- **Step 6:** Compile a total cost breakdown (property + legal + financing + moving + utilities).
- **Step 7:** Share condo preferences and budget information with Alex to ensure alignment.

4) **Data Planning (information needed from environment)**
- Retrieve user’s full name and contact info.
- Retrieve Alex’s contact info (to share preferences and budget).
- Retrieve any previous real estate or mortgage history (if available) to inform financing options.
- Retrieve user’s current financial capability or pre-approval status (if available).
- Retrieve any existing communication or email threads with Alex about condo planning to ensure consistency.

5) **Anticipated Changes**
- The exact condo listings may change based on availability and pricing from the real estate agent.
- Financing terms may vary depending on lender offers and user/Alex credit profiles.
- Legal and moving service costs may be adjusted once property details are finalized.
- User and Alex may refine preferences after reviewing the first set of listings (e.g., favoring a specific neighborhood or feature).

</initial_plan>
